				right_side = TUR_government_committee_struggle_government
				set_value = 0.3
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_continue_non_partisan_governments_tt
		}
		completion_reward = {
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = democratic

			}

				ideology = neutrality
				popularity = 0.05
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_elections = no }
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = neutrality
					elections_allowed = yes
				}
				set_country_flag = TUR_continue_non_partisan_governments
			}

				id = TUR_government_committee_struggle
				left_side = TUR_government_committee_struggle_committee
				right_side = TUR_government_committee_struggle_government
				set_value = 0.3
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_continue_non_partisan_governments_tt
			add_to_variable = { TUR_sce_stability_factor = 0.03 }
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			base = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
